// CoreMedia Cookies
delete_cookie("cmLocationTaxonomiesCookie", "/", ".emerson.com");
delete_cookie("cmKeywordCookie", "/", ".emerson.com");
delete_cookie("cmSubjectTaxonomiesCookie", "/", ".emerson.com");
delete_cookie("cmLastVisited", "/", ".emerson.com");
delete_cookie("cmReferrerCookie", "/", ".emerson.com");
delete_cookie("EMR_INFERRED_LOCALE", "/", ".emerson.com");
delete_cookie("EMR_CURRENT_SITE", "/", ".emerson.com");

function delete_cookie(name, path, domain) {
if (get_cookie(name)) {
document.cookie = name + "=\"toBeDeleted\"" +
((path) ? ";path=" + path : "") +
((domain) ? ";domain=" + domain : "") +
";expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT";
}
}
function get_cookie(cname) {
var name = cname + "=";
var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
var c = ca[i];
while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
c = c.substring(1);
}
if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
}
}
return "";
}
